if (!is_file('dev/vendor_update.sh')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/vendor_update.sh');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('dev/vendor_update.sh')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/vendor_update.sh');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') != '86e78957404ea97c4ee3501ed94554fc9245a91c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/vendor_update.sh');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/vendor_update.sh', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/vendor_update.sh');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== '86e78957404ea97c4ee3501ed94554fc9245a91c') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== 'bb21cb60dac35ac77a2a18f1812683ae4827d2f2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/vendor_update.sh');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/vendor_update.sh');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/vendor_update.sh')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/vendor_update.sh', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== '86e78957404ea97c4ee3501ed94554fc9245a91c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/vendor_update.sh');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt') != '058ff4b707d1d4e5425751ada39a54924e5fb140') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt') !== '058ff4b707d1d4e5425751ada39a54924e5fb140') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt') !== 'ecd83c9f1d0374d6e5e73de28a95afbe28c616dd') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt') !== '058ff4b707d1d4e5425751ada39a54924e5fb140') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/php7_compat.txt');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != 'b76d9365d5058193939e2868ffb6f64177fa90d1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'b76d9365d5058193939e2868ffb6f64177fa90d1') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'f12cfd33bd71e24c3822bcd65582583c7a749830') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'b76d9365d5058193939e2868ffb6f64177fa90d1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != 'f30d4e6ee6e8c2f2b1af434d2777b3a87f46dffe') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== 'f30d4e6ee6e8c2f2b1af434d2777b3a87f46dffe') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '0da5a0fb4752fa3a42d076d43840cbdb804d4b13') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== 'f30d4e6ee6e8c2f2b1af434d2777b3a87f46dffe') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') != '19e0f7c551f9c31fec120b8f7070778b61d7e89d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus.inc.php', 0644)) {

	}

			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus.inc.php', $backup_name)) {

			}

		writefile_6();

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '187c3b2206f63877b93f33710a0c786f91f3f76a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '187c3b2206f63877b93f33710a0c786f91f3f76a') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2dfdc528043bbdb0cf6ea42c59415aa0bf446525') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '187c3b2206f63877b93f33710a0c786f91f3f76a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
